 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="right"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center">


<IMG SRC="g418261img.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>AMAZON.COM ANNOUNCES THIRD QUARTER SALES UP 27% TO $13.81 BILLION </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">SEATTLE&#151;(BUSINESS WIRE)&#151;October 25, 2012&#151;Amazon.com, Inc. (NASDAQ: AMZN) today announced financial results for its third quarter ended
September&nbsp;30, 2012. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Operating cash flow increased 8% to $3.37 billion for the trailing twelve months, compared with $3.11 billion for
the trailing twelve months ended September&nbsp;30, 2011. Free cash flow&nbsp;decreased 31% to $1.06 billion for the trailing twelve months, compared with $1.53 billion for the trailing twelve months ended September&nbsp;30, 2011. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Common shares outstanding plus shares underlying stock-based awards totaled 469&nbsp;million on September&nbsp;30, 2012, consistent with 469&nbsp;million
one year ago. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Net sales increased 27% to $13.81 billion in the third quarter, compared with $10.88 billion in third quarter 2011. Excluding
the $348 million unfavorable impact from year-over-year changes in foreign exchange rates throughout the quarter, net sales grew 30% compared with third quarter 2011. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Operating loss was $28 million in the third quarter, compared with operating income of $79 million in third quarter 2011. The unfavorable impact from year-over-year changes in foreign exchange rates
throughout the quarter on operating loss was $3 million. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Net loss was $274 million in the third quarter, or $0.60 per diluted share, compared
with net income of $63 million, or $0.14 per diluted share, in third quarter 2011. The third quarter 2012 includes a loss of $169 million, or $0.37 per diluted share, related to our equity-method share of the losses reported by LivingSocial,
primarily attributable to its impairment charge of certain assets, including goodwill. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;Our approach is to work hard to charge
less.&nbsp;Sell devices near breakeven and you can pack a lot of sophisticated hardware into a very low price point,&#148; said Jeff Bezos, founder and CEO of Amazon.com.&nbsp;&#147;And our approach is working &#151; the $199 Kindle Fire HD is the
#1 bestselling product across Amazon worldwide.&nbsp;Incredibly, this is true even as measured by unit sales.&nbsp;The next two bestselling products worldwide are our Kindle Paperwhite and our $69 Kindle.&nbsp;We&#146;re selling more of each of
these devices than the #4 bestselling product, book three of the Fifty Shades of Grey series.&nbsp;And we haven&#146;t even started shipping our best tablet &#151; the $299 Kindle Fire HD 8.9&#148; ships November 20.&#148; </FONT></P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Worldwide Electronics and Other General Merchandise sales grew 36% to $8.56 billion. Excluding the unfavorable impact from year-over-year changes in
foreign exchange rates throughout the quarter, sales grew 39%. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The NASDAQ OMX Group announced the launch of FinQloud, a cloud computing offering powered by AWS and exclusively designed for the financial services
industry. FinQloud provides efficient management and storage of financial data to help market participants streamline operations and meet regulatory compliance requirements without making costly capital expenditures for their underlying
infrastructure. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

performance computing capabilities. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

endeavors to offer its customers the lowest possible prices. Amazon.com and other sellers offer millions of unique new, refurbished and used items in categories such as Books; Movies, Music&nbsp;&amp; Games; Digital Downloads; Electronics&nbsp;&amp;
Computers; Home&nbsp;&amp; Garden; Toys, Kids&nbsp;&amp; Baby; Grocery; Apparel, Shoes&nbsp;&amp; Jewelry; Health&nbsp;&amp; Beauty; Sports&nbsp;&amp; Outdoors; and Tools, Auto&nbsp;&amp; Industrial. Amazon Web Services provides Amazon&#146;s
developer customers with access to in-the-cloud infrastructure services based on Amazon&#146;s own back-end technology platform, which developers can use to enable virtually any type of business. Kindle Paperwhite is the most-advanced e-reader ever
constructed with 62% more pixels and 25% increased contrast, a patented built-in front light for reading in all lighting conditions, extra-long battery life, and a thin and light design. The new latest generation Kindle, the lightest and smallest
Kindle, now features new, improved fonts and faster page turns. Kindle Fire HD features a stunning custom high-definition display, exclusive Dolby audio with dual stereo speakers, high-end, laptop-grade Wi-Fi with dual-band support and
dual-antennas/MIMO for 40% faster throughput than other tablets, enough storage for HD content, and the latest generation processor and graphics engine&#151;and it is available in two display sizes&#151;7&#148; and 8.9&#148;. The large-screen Kindle
Fire HD is also available with 4G wireless, and comes with a groundbreaking $49.99 introductory 4G LTE data package. The all-new Kindle Fire features a 20% faster processor, 40% faster performance, twice the memory, and longer battery life.

<FILENAME>d418261dex992.htm
<DESCRIPTION>INFORMATION REGARDING NON-GAAP FINANCIAL MEASURES
<TEXT>
<HTML><HEAD>
<TITLE>INFORMATION REGARDING NON-GAAP FINANCIAL MEASURES</TITLE>
</HEAD>
 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="right"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Exhibit 99.2 </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Non-GAAP Financial Measures </I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Regulation G, <I>Conditions for Use of
Non-GAAP Financial Measures</I>, and other SEC regulations define and prescribe the conditions for use of certain non-GAAP financial information. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Our measure of &#147;Free cash flow&#148; meets the definition of a non-GAAP financial measure. Free cash flow is used in addition to and in conjunction with results presented in accordance with GAAP and
free cash flow should not be relied upon to the exclusion of GAAP financial measures. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Free cash flow, which we reconcile to
&#147;Net cash provided by (used in) operating activities,&#148; is cash flow from operations reduced by &#147;Purchases of fixed assets, including internal-use software and website development.&#148; We use free cash flow, and ratios based on it,
to conduct and evaluate our business because, although it is similar to cash flow from operations, we believe it typically will present a more conservative measure of cash flows since purchases of fixed assets are a necessary component of ongoing
operations. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Free cash flow has limitations due to the fact that it does not represent the residual cash flow available for
discretionary expenditures. For example, free cash flow does not incorporate payments made on capital lease obligations or cash payments for business acquisitions. Therefore, we believe it is important to view free cash flow as a complement to our
entire consolidated statements of cash flows. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">For a quantitative reconciliation of free cash flow to the most directly
comparable amounts reported in accordance with GAAP, see &#147;Supplemental Financial Information and Business Metrics&#148; in Exhibit 99.1 to this Current Report on Form&nbsp;8-K. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;Return on Invested Capital&#148; is a ratio based on free cash flow, and as such, is also a non-GAAP financial measure.&nbsp;Return
on invested capital is trailing twelve months free cash flow divided by average &#147;Total assets&#148; minus &#147;Current liabilities&#148; (excluding the current portion, if any, of our Long Term Debt), over the most recent five quarter
ends.&nbsp;We believe return on invested capital is a useful measure in assessing whether we are utilizing our capital efficiently.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">As with free cash flow, return on invested capital is used in addition to and in conjunction with results presented in accordance with GAAP and return on invested capital should not be relied upon to the
exclusion of GAAP financial measures.&nbsp;We include return on invested capital, and the denominator used to calculate it (called &#147;Invested Capital&#148;) in &#147;Supplemental Financial Information and Business Metrics&#148; in Exhibit 99.1
to this Current Report on Form&nbsp;8-K.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The effect on our consolidated statements of operations from changes in exchange
rates versus the U.S.&nbsp;Dollar is also a non-GAAP financial measure. Information regarding the effect of exchange rates, versus the U.S.&nbsp;Dollar, on our consolidated statements of operations is provided to show reported period operating
results had the exchange rates remained the same as those in effect in the comparable prior year period. We include various measures on both an as-reported basis and a basis showing the effect of changes in exchange rates versus the U.S. dollar in
&#147;Supplemental Financial Information and Business Metrics&#148; in Exhibit 99.1 to this Current Report on Form 8-K. </FONT></P>
</BODY></HTML>
</TEXT>
